    <p class="result"> 
<span class="pos Vn" style="color: #ff8000">Vn</span>n. techt, dul.</p>
   
    <p class="result"> 
MEANINGS.</p>
   
    <p class="result"> 
<span class="trans">
        <span class="def">Goes</span>, <span class="def">proceeds</span>
      </span>. Used absolutely, with accus., and with 
adverbs and prepositions particularising the meaning.</p>
   
    
      <p class="result"> 
<span class="edilb">I</span> Absolute uses.</p>
     
      
        <p class="result">(<span class="edilb">a</span>) <span class="trans">
            <span class="def">proceeds</span>, <span class="def">goes forward</span>, <span class="def">turns out</span>
          </span>: 
nā rega in dál sin `<span class="quote">that respite shall not be given</span>,' 
            <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/MacCongl." title="eDIL Bibliography">MacCongl.</strong></span> 
29.5
          . coná d'athchlaind mar dochúaid `<span class="quote">as it was no case 
of an inferior line</span>,' 
            <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/Metr.Dinds." title="eDIL Bibliography">Metr. Dinds.</strong></span> iv 260.31
          . maith dochuaidh 
críoch a bhagair `<span class="quote">well did his bluster succeed</span>,' 
            <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/TD" title="eDIL Bibliography">TD</strong></span> 3.37
          . </p>
      
     
      <p class="result"> 
(<span class="edilb">b</span>) <span class="trans">
          <span class="def">goes away</span>, <span class="def">departs</span>:</span> o dochóid in t-aingel <span class="ediltr">when the angel 
departed</span>, 
          <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/PH" title="eDIL Bibliography">PH</strong></span> 3470
        . téid iar sin `<span class="quote">thereupon he departs</span>,' 

          <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/&#xC9;riu" title="eDIL Bibliography">Ériu</strong></span> xii 188.5
        . airc-seo a Eochaid lat ainfiuss `<span class="quote">be off with 
thy ignorance</span>,' 
          <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/&#xC9;riu" title="eDIL Bibliography">Ériu</strong></span> viii 157.1
        .</p>
     
      
        <p class="result">(<span class="edilb">c</span>) <span class="trans">
            <span class="def">passes away</span>, <span class="def">vanishes</span>:</span> 
madh ro bhui aige in tan do rinne in cunnradh, ocus do 
chuaidh fri dethbirius `<span class="quote">if he had it (the property) when he 
made the contract and it passed away from him by necessity</span>,' 

            <span><strong class="pop" style="color:blue" href="bibliography/Laws" title="eDIL Bibliography">Laws</strong></span> iv 38.3 Comm.

<script>

	  $(document).ready( function() {

	  	$('#content').on('click', '.pop', function() {
	  		$.ajax({
	            context: this,  // set the context of the callbacks
	            type: "GET",
	            url:  $(this).attr('href'),
	            success: function(data) {
	            	$(this).popover({
	            		placement: function (context, source) {
					        var position = $(source).position();
					        if (position.left > 515) {
					            return "left";
					        }
					        if (position.left < 515) {
					            return "right";
					        }
					        if (position.top < 110){
					            return "bottom";
					        }
					        return "top";
						},
				        content: data,
				        title: 'Bibliography',
				        html: true,
	            	}).popover('show');
	            }
        	});
	  	});

		$('body').on('click', function (e) {
            $('.pop').each(function () {
                //the 'is' for buttons that trigger popups
                //the 'has' for icons within a button that triggers a popup
                if (!$(this).is(e.target) && $(this).has(e.target).length === 0 && $('.popover').has(e.target).length === 0) {
                    $(this).popover('destroy');
                }
            });
        });
	  })
</script>
